country_event = {
	id = kirin.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin.1"}
	title = kirin.1.t
	desc = kirin.1.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kirin.1.a
		add_political_power = 70
		set_country_flag = KIR_pol_1_available
		add_ideas =  KIR_pol_1
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_silence_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_stabilityWeeklyX_tt
		set_variable = { var = KIR_the_silence_weekly_stability_var value = -0.01 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin.10"}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		}

			ideology = communism

			name = KIR_communism_party_1 
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_plenum_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_stability1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_stab_var value = 0.01 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_plenum_communist1_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_shuffle_pol_advisors_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = KIR_pol_4
		set_country_flag = KIR_pol_4_available
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_communism_var value = 0.1 }
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_1_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_2_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_3_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_4_removable
		}
		set_country_flag = KIR_did_not_expel_communists
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kirin.10.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_unlock_entry_autumn_blaze
		add_to_variable = { KIR_diary_SG_protag_1_button_var = 1 }
		meta_effect = {
		  text = {
			set_variable = { KIR_diary_SG_protag_1_entry_[IDKIRX]_var = 3 }
			set_variable = { KIRDiary1Entry[IDKIRX]TitleVar = 3 }
		  }
		  IDKIRX = "[?KIR_diary_SG_protag_1_button_var|0]"
		}
		KIR_unlock_entry_effect = yes
		KIR_diary_SG_protag_1_button_click_effect = yes
		set_country_flag = KIR_expelled_communists
	}
}

					KIR_kindling_flash = { set_nationality = KIR }
					KIC_ember_glow = { set_nationality = KIR }
				}
			}

					is_owned_by = KIS
				}
				add_core_of = KIS
				remove_core_of = KIR
				add_claim_by = KIR
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_kiria_country = yes
				}
				news_event = { id = kirin_news.18 days = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
	title = kirin.105.t
	desc = kirin.105.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {

				limit = {

						is_ai = no
					}
				}

						count = 2

			NOT = {
				has_war_with = KIS
			}
			OR = {

				is_subject_of = ROOT
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
		}
		KIC = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = KIS
			}
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				has_capitulated = yes
				has_country_flag = KIC_fled_to_taungpau
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kirin_council.50.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_council_50_tt
		set_country_flag = KIS_unlock_empire_focus_tree
		hidden_effect = {
			load_focus_tree = { tree = KIR_council_empire_focus_tree keep_completed = yes }
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIS_viceroyalty_formed_flag
				}
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					character = "KIR_fickle_current"
					ideology = oligarchism
				}
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					character = "KIR_ardent_bloom"
					ideology = corporatocracy
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 64
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism 
					long_name = KIR_fascism_party_1_long
					name = KIR_fascism_party_1 
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality 
					long_name = KIR_fascism_party_3_long
					name =  KIR_fascism_party_3
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KIS = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = KIR_rhapsody_arsenal_available
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
			set_country_flag = KIR_rhapsody_arsenal_available
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
			show_ideas_tooltip = KIR_rhapsody_arsenal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIS_chose_griffonian_investors_flag
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KIS_griffonian_debts
				days = 90
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIS_chose_changeling_investors_flag
				CHN = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
			country_event = { id = kirin_council.72 days = 7 }
		}
	}

		set_variable = { KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level = 1073.industrial_complex_level }
		set_variable = { KIR_loot_cities_1073_mil_level = 1073.arms_factory_level }

			1059 = {
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_civ_level
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = arms_factory 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level
				}
			}
			1073 = {
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = arms_factory 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_mil_level
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = dockyard 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_nav_level
				}
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_civ_level > 0 }

				random_owned_controlled_state = {

					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_civ_level = 1 }
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level = 1 }
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level = 1 }
			}
			while_loop_effect = {

				set_variable = { COC_11_var = 0 } #done
				set_variable = { COC_12_var = 0.05 }
				set_variable = { COC_13_var = 0.05 }
				set_variable = { COC_14_var = 0 } ##Morale - done
				set_variable = { COC_15_var = 0.3 }
				set_variable = { COC_16_var = 0.3 }
				set_variable = { COC_17_var = 0 } ##Breakthrough - done
				set_variable = { COC_8_var = 0 } ##Terrain Penalty

					limit = {

					}
				}

							has_country_flag = KIS_council_salvation_front_civil_war_scenario
						}
					}
					KIR = {
						PREV = {
							transfer_technology = yes 
							transfer_society_ideas = yes
							transfer_science_ideas = yes
							transfer_poverty_ideas = yes
							transfer_illiteracy_ideas = yes
						}
					}
				}

					is_locked = yes

			}
		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = KIC_event_73_tt
	}

				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					check_variable = { KIC.FRV_crisis_averted_var > 1 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { FRV_crisis_averted_var = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_test.6 ##Randomise Banner Configuration
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_test.6"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = ROOT.controlled_states
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = FlagCoreVarRandom
				distribution = uniform
				min = 1
				max = 6
			}
			round_temp_variable = FlagCoreVarRandom
			set_variable = { FlagCoreVar = FlagCoreVarRandom }
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = FlagBorderVarRandom
				distribution = uniform
				min = 1
				max = 10
			}
			round_temp_variable = FlagBorderVarRandom
			set_variable = { FlagBorderVar = FlagBorderVarRandom }
		}
	}
}
